thing therein within three dayes one companie selfe restored fro death best knight world likewise whome tell ye violently caryed away knight ridden intending force heere must obserue damosell talking amadis knew reason helmet beuer couered face heard casket taken neuer left gallopping till ouertooke whome thus spake knight deale courteously giuing lady cause thus complaine think doo great deale better deliuer casket againe tooke knight heard fell great laughter doo ye thus laugh sir said amadis laugh answered knight whome thinke scant wise giuing councell demaunds lesse hope may haue speeding sute may quoth amadis care word yet good deliuer thing none belike threaten sayd knight sir answered amadis ouermuch boldnes vsing force ought true quoth knight word set casket aside tree returning amadis said brauerie deedes seemeth word come teach knowe receiue lawe giuing spurres horsses encountred together sort knight dismounted horsse fell heauily able rise againe meane amadis fetched cofer deliuering damosell said take owne faire lady tary heere till bring companion presently posted knight ouertaking thicket tree tyed horsse ladyes trayling haire head wood commit villainous desire amadis cried aloud manner euill death mayst thou dye traitour wrongest lady sort without offending thee knight strougled get wood looked vp sawe amadis whereupon left making speed weapon mounted horsseback approching neerer prince said hand knight haplesse time thee didst thou hinder answered amadis distaineth honor men beast despise take reuenge quoth knight let neuer weare armour againe world therein shall sustaine great losse replyed amadis one addicted villainy seekes force lady ought libertie honor defended loyall knight braue course met together though knight brake launce yet hurled ground violently weight armour strength fall made lye trembling traunce amadis perceiuing rid paine altogether trampled belly horsse feete saying thus shalt thou loose thy desire forcing ladyes faire soule hope heereafter rid daunger thanke lord quoth would god companyon hath lost casket well deliuered first met withall answered amadis wherefore first succoured well hath recouered taken behold squire conducteth hitherward heate somewhat violent amadis put helmet take aire damosell immediatly knew returne gaule conducted vrganda vnknowne whe chiualrie deliuered freend sweet uirgins replyed amadis remember humble dutie health mistresse telling knowes right well knight mander rode damoselles one way amadis another wherfore must tell happened arcalaus since departure
